                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  Plot@1100527350 : Record 11012500;
                                BEGIN
                                  TESTFIELD("Bill-to Customer No.");

                                  IF "Work Order"."Plot No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF Plot.GET("Work Order"."Source No.", "Work Order"."Plot No.") THEN
                                      FormatAddress.Plot(ProjectAddr, Plot);
                                  END ELSE
                                    FormatAddress.Project(ProjectAddr, Job);

                                  Customer.GET("Bill-to Customer No.");
                                  FormatAddress.Customer(CustomerAddr, Customer);

                                  IF NOT CurrReport.PREVIEW AND "Small Project" THEN
                                    IF "Small Project Status" < "Small Project Status"::Printed THEN BEGIN
                                      "Small Project Status" := "Small Project Status"::Printed;
                                      MODIFY;
                                    END;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=No.=FIELD(Source No.) }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value = 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Shared offset As Integer
Shared newgroup As Object
Shared currentgroup1 As Object

Public Function GetGroupPageNumber(newgroup2 As Boolean, pagenumber As Integer) As Object
    If newgroup2
        offset = pagenumber - 1
    End If
    Return pagenumber - offset
End Function

Public Function InNewGroup(group1 As Object) As Boolean
    newgroup = False
    If Not (group1 = currentgroup1)
        newgroup = True
        currentgroup1 = group1
    End If
    Return newgroup
End Function

Shared Data1 As Object

Public Function GetData(Num As Integer) As Object
    Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1), Chr(177))))
End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData As Object)
    If NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
        Data1 = NewData
    End If
End Function
</Code>
